$q(document).ready(function ()
{
    var viewed_items = function (id, items)
    {
        var ids = [];
        for (var i in items)
        {
            if (items[i] === id)
            {
                continue;
            }
            ids.push(items[i]);
        }
        return ids;
    };
    
    var add_to_storage = function (prod_id, items)
    {
        var pos = pos_in(prod_id, items);
        
        if (pos >= 0)
        {
            items.splice(pos, 1);
        }
        
        items.unshift(prod_id);
        
        if (items.length > 10)
        {
            items.splice(10);
        }
        
        U_storage.set(storage_name, items.toString());
        
        return items;
    };
    
    var pos_in = function (prod_id, items)
    {
        for (var i in items)
        {
            if (items[i] === prod_id)
            {
                return i;
            }
        }
        return -1;
    };
    
    try
    {
        if (!U_storage.inited)
        {
            return;
        }
        
        var storage_name = 'viewed_items';
        var prod_id      = "";
        
        if (parseInt(prod_id, 10) <= 0)
        {
            return;
        }
        
        var items = U_storage.get(storage_name) || '';
        items     = (items.length ? items.split(',') : []);
        
        if (items.length === 0)
        {
            add_to_storage(prod_id, items);
            return;
        }
        
        var post = {};
        
        post['b_ajax']              = true;
        post['submit_viewed_items'] = true;
        post['ui_items']            = viewed_items(prod_id, items); //рисуем всех, кроме текущего
        var qty                     = post['ui_items'].length;
        
        if (qty === 0)
        {
            return;
        }
        
        add_to_storage(prod_id, items); //добавляем текущий товар
        
        var $vieweditems = $q('#vieweditems');
        if (!$vieweditems.length)
        {
            return; //на странице нет отображения "вы уже смотрели"
        }
        
        $q.ajax({type: "POST", dataType: "json", url: '/', data: post})
        .done(function (result)
        {
            if (result.data === false)
            {
                return;
            }
            
            $vieweditems.html(result.html);
            
            var recommendedSlider = $vieweditems.find('._js_recommended-slider');
            initilizeSlickSlider(recommendedSlider);
            
            qty = result.TMPCounter['g_ids'].length; //подсчитываем пришедшие от сервера товары
            if (recommendedSlider.hasClass('_js_recommended-main') && qty < 4 && qty > 1)	//если товаров мало - отображать справа, для главной
            {
                recommendedSlider.find('.slick-track').css({'float': 'right'})
            }
            
            if (window.TMPCounter && result.TMPCounter && result.TMPCounter.block)
            {
                window.TMPCounter.block = window.TMPCounter.block.concat(result.TMPCounter.block);
                window.GTMConfig && window.GTMConfig.emit_load(result.TMPCounter.block);
            }
        });
    }
    catch (e)
    {
    }
});
